class \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_d_g_m_r_e_s}{DGMRES}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} Restarted \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_g_m_r_e_s}{GMRES} with deflation. This class implements a modification of the \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_g_m_r_e_s}{GMRES} solver for sparse linear systems. The basis is built with modified Gram-\/\+Schmidt. At each restart, a few approximated eigenvectors corresponding to the smallest eigenvalues are used to build a preconditioner for the next cycle. This preconditioner for deflation can be combined with any other preconditioner, the \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_incomplete_l_u_t}{Incomplete\+LUT} for instance. The preconditioner is applied at right of the matrix and the combination is multiplicative. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde} 
typedef \mbox{\hyperlink{tensor__benchmarks_8h_a23fafe2bd4e27ecadab4deb95691bcf4}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEFAULT\+\_\+\+DENSE\+\_\+\+INDEX\+\_\+\+TYPE}} Eigen\+::\+Index}



The \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index} type as used for the API. 

To change this, {\ttfamily \#define} the preprocessor symbol {\ttfamily EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEFAULT\+\_\+\+DENSE\+\_\+\+INDEX\+\_\+\+TYPE}. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\textbackslash{}blank \doxylink{TopicPreprocessorDirectives}{Preprocessor directives}, Storage\+Index. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{EulerAxis@{EulerAxis}!Eigen@{Eigen}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EulerAxis}{EulerAxis}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_ae614aa7cdd687fb5c421a54f2ce5c361} 
enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_eigen_ae614aa7cdd687fb5c421a54f2ce5c361}{Eigen\+::\+Euler\+Axis}}}



Representation of a fixed signed rotation axis for \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_euler_system}{Euler\+System}. 

\doxylink{sparse__setter_8cpp_a7c28d0550a40521b5d19a8a7bc029cd1}{Values} here represent\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The axis of the rotation\+: X, Y or Z.
\item The sign (i.\+e. direction of the rotation along the axis)\+: positive(+) or negative(-\/)
\end{DoxyItemize}

Therefore, this could express all the axes \{+X,+Y,+Z,-\/X,-\/Y,-\/Z\}

For positive axis, use +EULER\+\_\+\{axis\}, and for negative axis use -\/EULER\+\_\+\{axis\}. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}[2]{枚举值}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{EULER\_X@{EULER\_X}!Eigen@{Eigen}}\index{Eigen@{Eigen}!EULER\_X@{EULER\_X}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_eigen_ae614aa7cdd687fb5c421a54f2ce5c361a11e1ea88cbe04a6fc077475d515d0b38}\label{namespace_eigen_ae614aa7cdd687fb5c421a54f2ce5c361a11e1ea88cbe04a6fc077475d515d0b38} 
EULER\+\_\+X&the X axis \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{EULER\_Y@{EULER\_Y}!Eigen@{Eigen}}\index{Eigen@{Eigen}!EULER\_Y@{EULER\_Y}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_eigen_ae614aa7cdd687fb5c421a54f2ce5c361aee756a2b63043248f3d83541386c266b}\label{namespace_eigen_ae614aa7cdd687fb5c421a54f2ce5c361aee756a2b63043248f3d83541386c266b}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_a81f796c95561b9847eb8a6b8ccfa3e7d} 
template$<$typename Arg\+ADerived, typename Arg\+BDerived, typename Arg\+XDerived$>$ \\
const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_cwise_ternary_op}{Eigen\+::\+Cwise\+Ternary\+Op}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1internal_1_1scalar__betainc__op}{Eigen\+::internal\+::scalar\+\_\+betainc\+\_\+op}}$<$ typename Arg\+XDerived\+::\+Scalar $>$, const Arg\+ADerived, const Arg\+BDerived, const Arg\+XDerived $>$ Eigen\+::betainc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_array_base}{Eigen\+::\+Array\+Base}}$<$ Arg\+ADerived $>$ \&}]{a}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_array_base}{Eigen\+::\+Array\+Base}}$<$ Arg\+BDerived $>$ \&}]{b}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_array_base}{Eigen\+::\+Array\+Base}}$<$ Arg\+XDerived $>$ \&}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\textbackslash{}cpp11 \begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of the coefficient-\/wise betainc({\itshape x}, {\itshape a}, {\itshape b}) to the given arrays.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function computes the regularized incomplete beta function (integral).

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
This function supports only float and double scalar types in c++11 mode. To support other scalar types, or float/double in non c++11 mode, the user has to provide implementations of betainc(\+T,\+T,\+T) for any scalar type T to be supported.
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cauchy\_max\_bound()}{cauchy\_max\_bound()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_aa6dcbc8ff39a5916783d9b2d25af90d1} 
template$<$typename Polynomial$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_num_traits}{Num\+Traits}}$<$ typename\+Polynomial\+::\+Scalar $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{boostmultiprec_8cpp_ad5abe8020ead32dcab5e3c15d6d7c30e}{\+::\+Real}} Eigen\+::cauchy\+\_\+max\+\_\+bound (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const Polynomial \&}]{poly}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a maximum bound for the absolute value of any root of the polynomial.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em poly} & \+: the vector of coefficients of the polynomial ordered by degrees i.\+e. poly\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} is the coefficient of degree i of the polynomial e.\+g. $ 1 + 3x^2 $ is stored as a vector $ [ 1, 0, 3 ] $.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{前置条件}
the leading coefficient of the input polynomial poly must be non zero 
\end{DoxyPrecond}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_ab9ddb420f8dd9f00bfea8df504cceae5} 
template$<$typename Polynomial$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_num_traits}{Num\+Traits}}$<$ typename\+Polynomial\+::\+Scalar $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{boostmultiprec_8cpp_ad5abe8020ead32dcab5e3c15d6d7c30e}{\+::\+Real}} Eigen\+::cauchy\+\_\+min\+\_\+bound (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const Polynomial \&}]{poly}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a minimum bound for the absolute value of any non zero root of the polynomial. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em poly} & \+: the vector of coefficients of the polynomial ordered by degrees i.\+e. poly\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} is the coefficient of degree i of the polynomial e.\+g. $ 1 + 3x^2 $ is stored as a vector $ [ 1, 0, 3 ] $. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Creates a random Partial Isometry matrix of given rank.

\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} partial isometry is a matrix all of whose singular values are either 0 or 1. This is very useful to test rank-\/revealing algorithms. 函数调用图\+:

template$<$typename Derived, typename Exponent\+Derived$>$ \\
const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_cwise_binary_op}{Eigen\+::\+Cwise\+Binary\+Op}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1internal_1_1scalar__igamma__op}{Eigen\+::internal\+::scalar\+\_\+igamma\+\_\+op}}$<$ typename Derived\+::\+Scalar $>$, const Derived, const Exponent\+Derived $>$ Eigen\+::igamma (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_array_base}{Eigen\+::\+Array\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$ \&}]{a}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_array_base}{Eigen\+::\+Array\+Base}}$<$ Exponent\+Derived $>$ \&}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\textbackslash{}cpp11 \begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of the coefficient-\/wise igamma({\itshape a}, {\itshape x}) to the given arrays.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function computes the coefficient-\/wise incomplete gamma function.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
This function supports only float and double scalar types in c++11 mode. To support other scalar types, or float/double in non c++11 mode, the user has to provide implementations of igammac(\+T,\+T) for any scalar type T to be supported.
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{namespace_eigen_a4e6cd3acfea39bcff3fa38e0de1226f5}\index{Eigen@{Eigen}!kroneckerProduct@{kroneckerProduct}}
\index{kroneckerProduct@{kroneckerProduct}!Eigen@{Eigen}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{kroneckerProduct()}{kroneckerProduct()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_a4e6cd3acfea39bcff3fa38e0de1226f5} 
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_kronecker_product_sparse}{Kronecker\+Product\+Sparse}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}} $>$ Eigen\+::kronecker\+Product (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base}{Eigen\+Base}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}} $>$ \&}]{a}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base}{Eigen\+Base}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}} $>$ \&}]{b}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Computes Kronecker tensor product of two matrices, at least one of which is sparse

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
If you want to replace a matrix by its Kronecker product with some matrix, do {\bfseries{NOT}} do this\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_eigen_aedd4b7cd1e324ed0769cac2701f4d050}{kroneckerProduct}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}},\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}});\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ bug!!!\ caused\ by\ aliasing\ effect}}

\end{DoxyCode}
 instead, use \doxylink{sparse__permutations_8cpp_abf03ad46cd5db5b4eabad69a86a13a6c}{eval()} to work around this\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_eigen_aedd4b7cd1e324ed0769cac2701f4d050}{kroneckerProduct}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}},\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}).eval();}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em a} & Dense/sparse matrix a \\
\hline
{\em b} & Dense/sparse matrix b \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
Kronecker tensor product of a and b, stored in a sparse matrix 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{namespace_eigen_aedd4b7cd1e324ed0769cac2701f4d050}\index{Eigen@{Eigen}!kroneckerProduct@{kroneckerProduct}}
\index{kroneckerProduct@{kroneckerProduct}!Eigen@{Eigen}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{kroneckerProduct()}{kroneckerProduct()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_aedd4b7cd1e324ed0769cac2701f4d050} 
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_kronecker_product}{Kronecker\+Product}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}} $>$ Eigen\+::kronecker\+Product (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix_base}{Matrix\+Base}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}} $>$ \&}]{a}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix_base}{Matrix\+Base}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}} $>$ \&}]{b}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Computes Kronecker tensor product of two dense matrices

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
If you want to replace a matrix by its Kronecker product with some matrix, do {\bfseries{NOT}} do this\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_eigen_aedd4b7cd1e324ed0769cac2701f4d050}{kroneckerProduct}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}},\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}});\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ bug!!!\ caused\ by\ aliasing\ effect}}

\end{DoxyCode}
 instead, use \doxylink{sparse__permutations_8cpp_abf03ad46cd5db5b4eabad69a86a13a6c}{eval()} to work around this\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_eigen_aedd4b7cd1e324ed0769cac2701f4d050}{kroneckerProduct}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}},\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}).eval();}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em a} & \doxylink{struct_eigen_1_1_dense}{Dense} matrix a \\
\hline
{\em b} & \doxylink{struct_eigen_1_1_dense}{Dense} matrix b \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
Kronecker tensor product of a and b 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{namespace_eigen_a2f490197e16df831683018e383e29346}\index{Eigen@{Eigen}!matrix\_sqrt\_quasi\_triangular@{matrix\_sqrt\_quasi\_triangular}}
\index{matrix\_sqrt\_quasi\_triangular@{matrix\_sqrt\_quasi\_triangular}!Eigen@{Eigen}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{matrix\_sqrt\_quasi\_triangular()}{matrix\_sqrt\_quasi\_triangular()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_a2f490197e16df831683018e383e29346} 
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_transform}{Matrix\+Type}}, typename Result\+Type$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} Eigen\+::matrix\+\_\+sqrt\+\_\+quasi\+\_\+triangular (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_transform}{Matrix\+Type}} \&}]{arg}{, }\item[{Result\+Type \&}]{result}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute matrix square root of quasi-\/triangular matrix. 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_transform}{Matrix\+Type}} & type of {\ttfamily arg}, the argument of matrix square root, expected to be an instantiation of the \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix}{Matrix} class template. \\
\hline
{\em Result\+Type} & type of {\ttfamily result}, where result is to be stored. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em arg} & argument of matrix square root. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em result} & matrix square root of upper Hessenberg part of {\ttfamily arg}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function computes the square root of the upper quasi-\/triangular matrix stored in the upper Hessenberg part of {\ttfamily arg}. Only the upper Hessenberg part of {\ttfamily result} is updated, the rest is not touched. See Matrix\+Base\+::sqrt() for details on how this computation is implemented.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
Matrix\+Square\+Root, Matrix\+Square\+Root\+Quasi\+Triangular 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
函数调用图\+:

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{matrix\_sqrt\_triangular()}{matrix\_sqrt\_triangular()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_ae51c91f920f6ea4a7f6f72caa1e8249f}

Compute matrix square root of triangular matrix. 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_transform}{Matrix\+Type}} & type of {\ttfamily arg}, the argument of matrix square root, expected to be an instantiation of the \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix}{Matrix} class template. \\
\hline
{\em Result\+Type} & type of {\ttfamily result}, where result is to be stored. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em arg} & argument of matrix square root. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em result} & matrix square root of upper triangular part of {\ttfamily arg}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Only the upper triangular part (including the diagonal) of {\ttfamily result} is updated, the rest is not touched. See Matrix\+Base\+::sqrt() for details on how this computation is implemented.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
the evaluation of the polynomial at x using stabilized Horner algorithm.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em poly} & \+: the vector of coefficients of the polynomial ordered by degrees i.\+e. poly\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} is the coefficient of degree i of the polynomial e.\+g. $ 1 + 3x^2 $ is stored as a vector $ [ 1, 0, 3 ] $. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em x} & \+: the value to evaluate the polynomial at. \\

\Hypertarget{namespace_eigen_ae3b47a13a0699f5dbaa0623c11333dca}\index{Eigen@{Eigen}!polygamma@{polygamma}}
\index{polygamma@{polygamma}!Eigen@{Eigen}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{polygamma()}{polygamma()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_ae3b47a13a0699f5dbaa0623c11333dca} 
template$<$typename DerivedN, typename DerivedX$>$ \\
const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_cwise_binary_op}{Eigen\+::\+Cwise\+Binary\+Op}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1internal_1_1scalar__polygamma__op}{Eigen\+::internal\+::scalar\+\_\+polygamma\+\_\+op}}$<$ typename Derived\+X\+::\+Scalar $>$, const DerivedN, const DerivedX $>$ Eigen\+::polygamma (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_array_base}{Eigen\+::\+Array\+Base}}$<$ DerivedN $>$ \&}]{n}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_array_base}{Eigen\+::\+Array\+Base}}$<$ DerivedX $>$ \&}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\textbackslash{}cpp11 \begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of the coefficient-\/wise polygamma({\itshape n}, {\itshape x}) to the given arrays.
\end{DoxyReturn}
It returns the {\itshape n} -\/th derivative of the digamma(psi) evaluated at {\ttfamily x}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
This function supports only float and double scalar types in c++11 mode. To support other scalar types, or float/double in non c++11 mode, the user has to provide implementations of polygamma(\+T,\+T) for any scalar type T to be supported.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
Eigen\+::digamma() 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{namespace_eigen_afbc3648f7ef67db3d5d04454fc1257fd}\index{Eigen@{Eigen}!roots\_to\_monicPolynomial@{roots\_to\_monicPolynomial}}
\index{roots\_to\_monicPolynomial@{roots\_to\_monicPolynomial}!Eigen@{Eigen}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{roots\_to\_monicPolynomial()}{roots\_to\_monicPolynomial()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_afbc3648f7ef67db3d5d04454fc1257fd} 
template$<$typename Root\+Vector, typename Polynomial$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} Eigen\+::roots\+\_\+to\+\_\+monic\+Polynomial (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const Root\+Vector \&}]{rv}{, }\item[{Polynomial \&}]{poly}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Given the roots of a polynomial compute the coefficients in the monomial basis of the monic polynomial with same roots and minimal degree. If Root\+Vector is a vector of complexes, Polynomial should also be a vector of complexes. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em rv} & \+: a vector containing the roots of a polynomial. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em poly} & \+: the vector of coefficients of the polynomial ordered by degrees i.\+e. poly\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} is the coefficient of degree i of the polynomial e.\+g. $ 3 + x^2 $ is stored as a vector $ [ 3, 0, 1 ] $. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_product}{Scalar}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} Flags, typename Storage\+Index$>$ \\

Returns a view of the Cholmod sparse matrix {\itshape cm} as an \doxylink{namespace_eigen}{Eigen} sparse matrix. The data are not copied but shared. \Hypertarget{namespace_eigen_af9555e27540da78d2c4bdd17d3b750b1}\index{Eigen@{Eigen}!zeta@{zeta}}
\index{zeta@{zeta}!Eigen@{Eigen}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{zeta()}{zeta()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_af9555e27540da78d2c4bdd17d3b750b1} 
template$<$typename DerivedX, typename DerivedQ$>$ \\
const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_cwise_binary_op}{Eigen\+::\+Cwise\+Binary\+Op}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1internal_1_1scalar__zeta__op}{Eigen\+::internal\+::scalar\+\_\+zeta\+\_\+op}}$<$ typename Derived\+X\+::\+Scalar $>$, const DerivedX, const DerivedQ $>$ Eigen\+::zeta (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_array_base}{Eigen\+::\+Array\+Base}}$<$ DerivedX $>$ \&}]{x}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_array_base}{Eigen\+::\+Array\+Base}}$<$ DerivedQ $>$ \&}]{q}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
an expression of the coefficient-\/wise zeta({\itshape x}, {\itshape q}) to the given arrays.
\end{DoxyReturn}
It returns the Riemann zeta function of two arguments {\itshape x} and {\itshape q\+:} 


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em x} & is the exposent, it must be \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 1 \\
\hline
{\em q} & is the shift, it must be \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
This function supports only float and double scalar types. To support other scalar types, the user has to provide implementations of zeta(\+T,\+T) for any scalar type T to be supported.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_array_base_ad996aade2210f810f1b11d43a611b1e3}{Array\+Base\+::zeta()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

const \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} Eigen\+::\+Coherent\+Access\+Pattern = 0x1}

\Hypertarget{namespace_eigen_ad81fa7195215a0ce30017dfac309f0b2}\index{Eigen@{Eigen}!Dynamic@{Dynamic}}
\index{Dynamic@{Dynamic}!Eigen@{Eigen}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Dynamic}{Dynamic}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_ad81fa7195215a0ce30017dfac309f0b2} 
const \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} Eigen\+::\+Dynamic = -\/1}

This value means that a positive quantity (e.\+g., a size) is not known at compile-\/time, and that instead the value is stored in some runtime variable.

Changing the value of Dynamic breaks the ABI, as Dynamic is often used as a template parameter for \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix}{Matrix}. \Hypertarget{namespace_eigen_a73c597189a4a99127175e8167c456fff}\index{Eigen@{Eigen}!DynamicIndex@{DynamicIndex}}
\index{DynamicIndex@{DynamicIndex}!Eigen@{Eigen}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{DynamicIndex}{DynamicIndex}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_a73c597189a4a99127175e8167c456fff} 
const \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} Eigen\+::\+Dynamic\+Index = 0xffffff}

This value means that a signed quantity (e.\+g., a signed index) is not known at compile-\/time, and that instead its value has to be specified at runtime. \Hypertarget{namespace_eigen_ab63002a89341ef7158fe60fa7570e88c}\index{Eigen@{Eigen}!expx@{expx}}

{\bfseries 初始值\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{=\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group__flags_gae4f56c2a60bbe4bd2e44c5b19cbe8762}{RowMajorBit}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ |\ \mbox{\hyperlink{group__flags_gaa34e83bae46a8eeae4e69ebe3aaecbed}{EvalBeforeNestingBit}}}

\end{DoxyCode}
\Hypertarget{namespace_eigen_a3163430a1c13173faffde69016b48aaf}\index{Eigen@{Eigen}!HugeCost@{HugeCost}}
\index{HugeCost@{HugeCost}!Eigen@{Eigen}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{HugeCost}{HugeCost}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_a3163430a1c13173faffde69016b48aaf} 
const \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} Eigen\+::\+Huge\+Cost = 10000}

This value means that the cost to evaluate an expression coefficient is either very expensive or cannot be known at compile time.

This value has to be positive to (1) simplify cost computation, and (2) allow to distinguish between a very expensive and very very expensive expressions. It thus must also be large enough to make sure unrolling won\textquotesingle{}t happen and that sub expressions will be evaluated, but not too large to avoid overflow. \Hypertarget{namespace_eigen_a7951593b031e13d90223c83d022ce99e}\index{Eigen@{Eigen}!Infinity@{Infinity}}
\index{Infinity@{Infinity}!Eigen@{Eigen}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Infinity}{Infinity}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_a7951593b031e13d90223c83d022ce99e} 
const \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} Eigen\+::\+Infinity = -\/1}

This value means +Infinity; it is currently used only as the p parameter to \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix_base_a3312bfc4fd6b398acdadecbcedf7a1fc}{Matrix\+Base\+::lp\+Norm$<$int$>$()}. The value Infinity there means the L-\/infinity norm. \Hypertarget{namespace_eigen_ad3a7fa97adf0db7055c92f466cecc271}\index{Eigen@{Eigen}!InnerRandomAccessPattern@{InnerRandomAccessPattern}}
\index{InnerRandomAccessPattern@{InnerRandomAccessPattern}!Eigen@{Eigen}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{InnerRandomAccessPattern}{InnerRandomAccessPattern}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_eigen_ad3a7fa97adf0db7055c92f466cecc271}
